# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
What the node represents depends on a specifc problem
It may include: 
- The state of input parameter
- The depth of the recursion tree
- Intermediate result ()
- The decision at that step
- Function return values:

 ^EbpuJ6AE

After the right node has been processed... ^Xjts6WIn

Before processing the node ^4Y2Np5zx

After processing the left child
or (before processing next child) ^hJy86imy
